 tippaniyan Comrade Pansare and his wife were shot dead by unidentified assailants while returning from Morning Walk on the day of February 16, 2015

 uttarakhand ke mukhyamantri trivendra singh ravat ne corbett or rajaji tigar rigerv main baaghon kii gananaa ke varsh 2016-17 ke taaje aankade jari kiye
 a minimum of 208 unique tigers have been identified in the Corbett Tiger Reserve and a minimum of 34 unique tigers in the Rajaji Tiger Reserve
 pichley varsh yah sankhya corbett tigar rigerv main 163 evam rajaji tigar rigerv main 16 pai gai thi
 The Chief Minister said that Uttarakhand has become the number one state in the country in terms of number of tigers in proportion to area with 340 tigers
 haalanki 400 baaghon kii sankhya ke saath karnataka ab bhi pehle sthaan par he
 535 cameras were installed in Corbett Tiger Reserve All ranges of Corbett Tiger Reserve had cameras installed on the basis of grid
 baaghon kii ginati ke liye lagbhag 535 camere lagaae gaye
 The tigers in Corbett Tiger Reserve were counted in two stages
 pehle charan kii gananaa 28 november, 2016 se 21 janvari, 2017 tak corbett tiger rigerv ke ramnagar tiger rigerv prabhag main camera trep vidhi ke madhyam se kii gai
 In the second phase, from January 25, 2017 to March 19, 2017, the Kalagarh Tiger Reserve Division was done through the camera
 prayek camere bindu par do camere lagaae gaye
 235 camera points were made in Ramnagar Tiger Reserve and cameras were placed for 55 days
 vahiin kalagarh tiger rigerv main 232 camere point par 54 dinon ke liye camere lagaae gaye
 Thus, 4,24,870 photographs were received from the total 25,453 trap nights of Corbett Tiger Reserve
 inamen kul 3892 tasviren baaghon kii milin
 2,539 photographs were used to count tigers
 baaghon kii ginati kii gai or tasviir ke baayen or daaen bhaag kaa milan kiya gaya
 In which left and right facets (flank) of 142 distinct tigers were found
 66 vishisht baaghon ke keval baayen pahalu praapt hue
 The tigers have been counted as the basis of the aspect
 96 baaghon ke daaen pahalu praapt hue
 These were not matched and were not included in the count
 corbett tiger rigerv ke antargat ramnagar tiger rigerv prabhag main 99 vishisht baaghon va 06 vishisht shavakon kii pahchaan kii gai tathaa kalagarh tiger rigerv prabhag main 109 vishisht baaghon kii pahchaan kii gai

 But on January 1 last year, when the Muni Prabal Sagar in Girnar, the holy shrine of the Jains in Junagadh district of Gujarat, was mortally attacked, like other tolerant people from all over the country, people of Jain religion also came to grief
 yah hamalaa us gujarat rajya main hua jahaan ke mukhyamantri pehle hi apni dharmik kattarta or alpsankhyakon ke prati katutapurna rukh ke liye jane jate hai
 And in this state of the country, Jain society did not even have the status of minority
 aise main centre sarkaar bhi unki bahut zyada madad karne kii haisiyat main nahin thi
 Similarly, in Lucknow, a statue of our adorable Tirthankara was broken in public
 idhar, mandiron se murti chori or jain santon par hamale bhi nirantar badhate rahe
 The religious leaders of Digambara, Shwetambara, Sthanakwasi and Terapanthi, all the four parts of the Jain society, were exacerbated by these circumstances and felt that it was necessary to give minority status to the Jain society for the protection of religion, the maintenance of faith and the protection of the sages
 is dard ko jitani gambhirtha se jain samaaj mahasoos kar rahaa tha, utani hi shiddat se congress adhyaksh sonia gandhi, rahul gandhi or mananeey pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne bhi samajha
 The Gandhi family has always been fond of Jainism, whether they were the first Prime Minister Panditji or the country's iron lady Indira Gandhi
 vartmaan netritv kii manshaa ko to khud mere udhaaharan se samajha ja saktaa he
 To represent Jain society in the Central Government, an activist like me, who has become a Member of Parliament for the first time, was given a place as a Minister in the Central Government
 rahul gandhi se samay-samay par jain samaaj ke sheershasth log milte rahe or unhen yah baat preshit kii ki jain samaaj ko alpsankhyak kaa darja dene kaa sahi vakt aa gaya he

 rahamaan khan ke saath hi kanoon mantri kapil sibbal ne cabinet main is prastaav ko sateek dhang se rakhane ke liye bahut mehnat kii
 i am personally very grateful to him for this
 main or jain samaaj yah jaanata he ki sirf kanoonee darja milane se jain samaaj kii sthiti raturaat nahin badal jaaegi
 But now society will have legal options to at least have its say
 agar narendra modi jaise alpsankhyak virdohi netaa ke shashan main utpaati log girnaar jaisaa cond dobaaraa karne kii jurrat karenge to kam-se-kam unhen alpsankhyak ayog ke kathghare main khadaa kiya ja sakegaa
 As far as the practical impact of this result of cannibet is concerned, Jain society is neither asking for reservation in jobs nor does it talk about minority status
 yani kisi bhi dharmik samaaj kaa haq maarane kii ratti bhar gunjaaish bhi jain samaaj nahin chahta
 The special privileges that the Jain society will get by getting this status - for example, it will increase the safety of the Jain community
 jis tarah baaki alpsankhyak dharm apni dharmik shiksha apane skulon ke jariye dete hai, ab vah kaam jain samaaj bhi kar sakegaa
 Most of the people of this community are associated with private business, in such a situation, they will also be provided loans at low interest and the facility of cheap technology and vocational education
 sabase badi baat yah ki jain collejon main jain bacchon ke liye 50 fisadi siten arakshit hongi
 The religious places, institutions, temples, pilgrimage areas and trusts of Jain religious people will not be able to be governmentized or acquired, but proper development and security of religious places will also be made by the government
 upasna sthal adhinium 1991 ( 42a k- 18-9-91) ke tahat kisi dharmik upasna sthal ko banaae rakhane ke liye spasht nirdesh honge, jiskaa ullaghann dhara 6(3) ke adheen dandaneey aparaadh he
 Property of trusts operated by the community will also be exempted from the Rent Control Act
 jain mandiron, tirth sthalon, shaikshanik sansthaaon ityadi ke prabandh kii jimmedaari samudaay ke haath main di jaaegi
 The government will provide all facilities and land at concessional rates to the Jain community to open schools, colleges, hostels, research or training institutes
 isse bhi badi baat yah ki jain samudaay kii ore se sanchalit jin sansthaaon par kanoon kii aad main bahusnkhyakon ne kabja jamaa rakhaa he unase mukti milegi
 The money donated by Jainism for virtue, zoological service, education etc
 will be tax free
 yah sab isliye bhi jaruri tha kyonki jain samudaay ke sadsy lakshadweep ko chhodkar desh ke har rajya main nivas karte hai
 The number of Jains is only 0 of the total number of the country
 4 fisadi he
 Long before government recognition, the courts of the country have been stamping this sentiment of the Jain community
 darasal, sari dikkat 1992 se shuru hui
 a notification was issued on 23 October 1993 under the National Minorities Commission Act 1992, made by the Central Government, and declared Muslim, Christian, Sikh, Buddhist and Parsi societies as religious minority societies
 lekin jain samaaj ko is suchi se baahar rakhaa gaya, jabaki 1973 se 1992 tak jain samaaj ko yah darja praapt tha
 Even before the present decision of the Central Government, the Jains enjoyed the status of state-level religious minority society in Chhattisgarh, Rajasthan, Haryana, Delhi, Uttar Pradesh, Madhya Pradesh, Karnataka, Maharashtra, Andhra Pradesh, West Bengal, Uttarakhand and Jharkhand
 vaise bhi desh main jis tarah sampradayik shaktiyaan sir uthaa rahi hai, usase hamen itihaas ke us daur ko nahin bhoolanaa chahie jab sabhi dharmon ne raashtra nirmaan main bhoomika nibhaai thi
 Jain society has always built dharamshalas and huge temples all over the country
 sabhi virgon ko swasthya sevaayen uplabdh karaane ke liye jain samaaj ke dhani-maani log hameshaa se prayaas karte rahe hai
 Now with the grant of minority status to their trusts, this work will be done on a wider scale
 hamaare paas sankhya bal itnaa nahin he ki ham paryaapt sankhya main apane samaaj ke vidhayak yaa saansad chun saken , jo samay aane par samaaj kii paramparaon, maryaadaaon or iske hiton ke sangrakshan ke liye aavashyak kanoon banavaa saken

 "today, Jain society has got its legal right with the intention of Rahul Gandhi
 lekin is nirnay ke saath hi jain samudaay kii jimmedaari bhi bad gai he

 iske baad aap is massej ko delit karen yaa naa bhi karen lekin aapaki lokation aapane stoker ko de di he

 ye link IP logar client ke jariye taiyaar kiye jate hai

 yaheen liks aapako massej ke rup main bheje jate hai or massej aise hote hai jinhen dekhakar aap clic karne par majaboor ho jaaen

 iske baad jasusi karne vaala IP trekar kii madad se aapaki lokation kii jaankaree ikatthi kar saktaa he

 Nehru's legacy Phulpur: After the first Lok Sabha elections were held in 1952, Pandit Jawaharlal Nehru chose the Phulpur parliamentary seat of Allahabad for his Karmabhoomi
 iske baad se lagaataar teen baar 1952, 1957 or 1962 main unhone phulpur se jeet darj kii thi

 haalanki wo jeet nahin sake
